<review>My co-worker and I found this place when we were going to the Thai place next door. We noticed the Pho shop and decided to give it a try, since it was a new restaurant for us and we both enjoy Pho.

The interior was casual, but not sloppy.  Very clean with a relaxed atmosphere.  The staff was helpful and always had a smile.

The Pho was very good, and the veggie plate was fresh and crisp.  The broth used was outstanding and the meat in my bowl was extremely tender and tasty.  I don't always find the meat in a bowl of Pho to be all that tasty at most Pho restaurants (maybe it's the way they cook the meat; maybe it's the fact that the meat has been boiling too long and has released all its flavor).

This Pho restaurant was an exception, as the meats were tender and flavorful.

My co-worker and I will definitely be back, as we have added this restaurant to our short-list of places to dine while in the Mountain View/Sunnyvale area.

The only reason I didn't give Luv Pho 5 full stars is that they do not offer a B√°nh m√¨ Sandwich, which is a wonderful sandwich to experience if you haven't.  Add some B√°nh m√¨ sandwiches to the menu and this would be the perfect Pho hot spot.< /review>< userid>

<user>102979844562643108300< /user>< text>
Excellent chaat and great service. Highly recommend the samosa chaat and paneer pakora.

Note: This is the original Delhi Chaat which was located at Old San Francisco Rd. They have a new location and new (blue) truck but it's still run by the same friendly owner.

Due to the various location changes over the last year, many old customers aren't aware that this food truck is still open, and unfortunately, some people confuse it with other chaat shops in the area.< /text>

<username>Erns Valdez<//username><Time>1543709875117< /Time><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
An absolute gem! An old church turned into an amazing restaurant. Beautiful entrance leads you to the back of the building to the patio area. Lovely and spacious with real artwork and a wall of herbs and plants that can be used in the kitchen. The restaurant interior is very impressive with its stained glass windows, large murals and small decor accents that bring new life to this old building. Modern with an old world vibe.

The cocktails are simple but enchanting in flavor and presentation. The food is absolutely amazing! Having sampled most of the menu I can tell you that each dish is beautiful, well thought out in preparation and presentation. Combinations of ingredients I haven't seen in other restaurants of this calibre and original takes on some familiar dishes. The high quality food is modestly priced which makes this a must and will for sure keep me coming back.< /Review>

<Name>Patrick Baumgartner<//Name>< Review>
These fools who work here; I'm surprised they knew how to put an apron on. My experience went as such: Waiting in line for what seemed an immense amount of time, for they were not busy, they finally served the man in front of me. The man placed his order for an earl grey latte, and the employees end up wasting five minutes arguing to each other how to make it correctly, and what the actual price is. Catching on some of the words, the man realized they had been overcharging him for that drink for some time now, which the employee admitted to. They kept arguing, and finally the man told them to stop bickering and to make his drink. So finally it was my turn: A black coffee. Not only were they snappy and rude to me (as arguing continued) It took several minutes for them to fill my order. Between arguing and playing on their phones, I don't understand how they function. The coffee when finally received was not hot, and had an awfully stale taste to it. I am surprised to see such things from Starbucks. Will not be returning to this store ever again, and I'd advice others not to support this branch.<//Review>

< Review>
Horrible business practices! In August 2017 I booked a rental house through Vacation Palm Springs for 5 days in April 2018. Now it's February 2018 and they cancelled the reservation on me, with only two months notice.

They haven't refunded my deposit yet, they haven't offered me any discount on another purchase and they refuse to accept blame. They cite that the homeowner sold his property and therefore they have absolutely no obligation to honor our existing rental contract. If I had cancelled on them I would still be charged 10% of the original contract; but apparently it is okay when they cancel on me instead. I put over $1,000 down on a deposit for a $4,200 rental agreement for a 5 bedroom property.

I will never ever use this company or recommend this company to anyone for any reason. They will ruin your vacation last minute and act like it's your fault.

Email message from Bunnie @ Vacation Palm Springs:
"The home you reserved [RENTAL HOME NAME] is no longer available for your dates.  The was sold.  I know that this is disappointing, but I am here to help.  Listed below are 5 bedroom homes that are open and available for your dates.  My contact information is listed below I will be in the office tomorrow morning from 9:00 am to 6:00 pm.  If you should see a home that you are interested please email me or you call me at the number listed tomorrow."

EDIT UPDATE:
Yes, Vacation Palm Springs did offer alternative houses - but not a single one of the alternatives they proposed matched the dates I had chosen. IE Every alternative they offered up would have me leaving a day earlier than was possible, and because I was in Palm Springs for a work trip, this was not an option. So in short, no, Vacation Palm Springs did not offer appropriate alternatives.

Further, the five alternatives that were sent to me clearly stated the daily rental rate, which was much higher than my original booking and out of my budget. I don't know if Vacation Palm Springs would have honored the original rates for the nicer rental homes, but when we are talking about a difference in the $2,000 to $6,000 range, it needs to be described to me, up front, that they would have honored that original booking rate. Explaining to me over Google Reviews that they would have honored the original rate is not acceptable.

Lastly, Yes, it is not in the terms and conditions of Vacation Palm Springs to guarantee availability of a property even when booked in advance. So, when I booked a property 9 months in advance and it was sold 2 months before my stay - they are not responsible nor liable based on their terms and conditions. This does not put the customer first, or guarantee an excellent experience.

Had I been offered realistic alternatives (IE alternative 5 bedroom rentals for the full duration of my intended stay) and been instructed that they would have honored the original price (instead of listing the higher rental price in their email) this would have been a 4 star listing. Instead, I was left with alternatives that didn't fit my schedule, or were out of my budget, and I had to frantically search for my own alternative houses for me and my 5 guests for our stay - the week before Coachella. I stand by my 1-star review because I feel that is what Vacation Palm Springs deserves. I was left without a rental home on short notice for one of the busiest weeks of the year, and was not treated promptly and fully with the respect I feel is deserved when booking a $4,200 rental home.</Review>

Let me begin by saying this company sent me a review form right after our departure in which I shared the following concerns and asked them to contact me by today-January 5, 2019-one week post departure if they did not want me to post on social media and contact the BBB.  I was sure they would want to address this privately and gave them the opportunity to do so. Nothing...not even an acknowledgement.  At the same time I posted the same review  information on the "El Paseo Modern" house we had rented directly on their website and waited for it to appear.  Of course, it did not.  Then it hit me...they only post positive reviews, which is why this house had not had a review posted for 6 months.

In their original inquiry, they asked what one thing would have made our stay better.  Here was my response: "It would be more like a dozen things that needed change and, moreover, required a great deal of assertiveness on our parts to have even some of them addressed on the 22nd (the day we checked in) versus the 26th (the day after Christmas)----which your staff stated was "because we are so busy and it is the holidays" which, of course, had we not pushed back, would have been more than half way through our stay.  The top dozen were: 1) pool and jacuzzi not heating or draining properly and not chlorinated properly, 2) gate code never worked, 3) ice maker not working, 4) trash compactor broken, 5) outside TV ripped off wall, 6) 4 of the outside lounges slashed and unusable, 7) dining room light broken, 8) no refrigerated water, 9) outside awning broken therefore no shade,10) BBQ hood missing left side screws so unusable for outside grilling 11) two of the dining room chairs unstable to sit in, 12) and refrigerator doors not closing properly (freezer had been left open upon our arrival because of this issue and all the ice trays melted).  Everywhere we looked during our first few hours of settling in, we found more things in poor condition and unaddressed maintenance issues.

When I finally got very firm with Alexis and Jade, which should not be necessary when we have paid top dollar and agreed to all terms thus fulfilling our end of the bargain, they sent Jose to "save the day"...he did as much as he could to bring things into the best working order on a Saturday night (we gave him a sizable tip for his efforts because of his work ethic and sincerity). However, many things remained undone because Jose's resources were limited---he could not fix an expensive awning or replace and rehang an expensive TV.

Our issue then became false advertising...both in photos and in print (we kept copies of what we were told we were getting from your website) given that we were told we would have all of these amenities, yet many were not there...yes, that is fraudulent...if things change with a rental home, you MUST amend your advertising or you must offer a rebate or the chance for us to cancel and be placed in a similar home close by...neither was done or offered. You do the owners an injustice (I do hope they themselves read this) if you do not manage their property within these ethical and legal boundaries.  The owners actually have a potentially lovely property, but they deserve to know what is being left undone and we deserve to have full disclosure if we are not going to get what was advertised and what we paid for. All of this was unfair, stressful, and really poor business practice on  "Vacation Palm Springs" company's part. I recommend you have full "informed consent", having toured and walked any property you are interested in renting, prior to doing so.< /Text>

We rented a property called "Sleek Retreat" in the Racquet Club area for five weeks in Feb/March 2018.
A nice house that needs to be freshened up. It's tired.
The carpets in all three bedrooms were filthy and heavily stained.
A towel rack was obviously torn from the wall in the main bathroom and the patch job appeared to have been done by a six year old.
The outdoor, fire pit furniture was well beyond it's "best before" date.
However our main complaint was the pool heater.
It rarely worked. We phoned the Palm Springs office on four occasions when we wanted to heat the pool and the heater didn't work. The first three times they sent someone around later in the day and the employee managed to get it working. Always too late in the day to actually use the pool as it takes some time to heat. On the final occasion I attended the office and demanded that they actually have the problem addressed by someone who could fix it as opposed to merely getting it temporarily running. I was told that I would be the top priority.
When no one had arrived four hours later, I phoned again, quite upset and they finally sent someone who fixed the heater. Once again too late to use that day.
When we checked out on March 15 we complained to a manager who said we would receive some credit for these issues.
We were charged an upfront deposit of $1,850 to cover gas/electrical we consumed during our stay, with the unused portion to be refunded.
Well, here it is a month later and we still haven't received our unused power refund back. Power consumption can be viewed in real time on the web. Pretty simple process.
We also paid an upfront cleaning fee of $225 for a house that we left much cleaner than we found when we arrived.
We have contacted the Palm Springs office a few times since we left and have been met with a lack of concern bordering on rudeness.
We also have placed calls to the company head office in New Jersey and they don't return calls, at least to us.
All in all, an experience that makes it highly unlikely that we will ever use the services of this company again.
We were also asked to review the property but I see that hasn't been posted which makes me feel they probably only post positive reviews associated with the specific properties.
As such, anyone relying on their posted reviews to assist in the decision to rent a property should be very cautious.
Dave Aitken
Vancouver<//review>

< Review>
The socially distanced line basically wrapped around the parking lot blocking in some cars. The parking lot is a bit cramped so beware. I went on a Friday at 12pm. I saw this long line though it was only about a 15minute wait. At the front of the line, they offer you a sanitized cart or basket. I wonder how Trader Joe's hire the same nice friendly personas for every employee at every location. There is plenty of room to socially distance in the store. I just wish they keep more of their most popular items in backstock and restock the shelves more often. But I guess that's how you keep the customers coming back.< /Review>

Austin C< /name>
<Review>- 98% of interactions with employees are pleasant and upbeat.

- Pricing has been incredibly fair and relatively competitive over the past decade

- Selection is consistent, but inventory depends on time of day

- Fresh non-refridgerated produce quality is seasonal; 75% of my visits come out with good quality produce, so long as you check before you buy.

- I recommend buying their non-bagged fruits when given a choice. Half the bagged alternatives are duds (has nothing to do with being labelled "organic" or not).

- About 2-4% of their fresh non-bagged fruit will have critical damage (bruises, punctures).

- The refridgerated and frozen foods are consistent and reliable.

- It should not go unstated that the Masonic Trader Joe's is always busy from 12pm to 9pm; the parking lot is always packed at this time, but there is always a traffic operator helping keep the lot flowing at a constant pace. At worst for the afternoons, the lane turning into the lot may take 10 minutes. Usually it's about 5 minutes or less. If you want to avoid any wait times, the only option is to go on a Sunday or weekday morning.

As the customer lines imply, there's nowhere else in the city that I would rather get my grocery shopping done.< /Review><Rate>5<//Rate><Gmap_id>0x8085873546aee719:0x968b0157ae6ea287< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<Pics>None< /Pics><Text>It's a little farther than others, but superior in price and convenience. Good, less-expensive  produce and dairy (including European unsweetened made with whole milk yogurt), nice packaged cheese selections. Seasonal Danish Kringle not available elsewhere. Pound plus chocolate bars are inexpensive but delicious, especially the 72%. Dried Montmorency cherries and raisins great in oatmeal. Nice fresh flowers. Artichoke jalapeno dip and garlic hummus. Woven wheat Triscuit alternative with less salt, and various chips varieties, good with the dips and cheese. Filet mignon is expensive but worth it. Two-Buck-Chuck (now more) is a favorite for their Merlot and White Zinfandel especially, better than more expensive wines. The Josephson's beer is quite good, and there are several varieties like Marzen, Heffeweisen, mild ale and bitter IPA. Good potstickers and other ethnic foods and desserts. The store is big enough for all the products, but not so big you have to walk all over the place, because they don't carry dozens of different brands of the same thing. I am truly glad there is a TJ's in walking distance.<//Text>< Resp>
